t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n846: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Mode = t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n847: \n848: \tif t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode == indexgateway.RingMode {\n849: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IngesterName = t.Cfg.Ingester.LifecyclerConfig.ID\n855: \n856: \t// If RF > 1 and current or upcoming index type is boltdb-shipper then disable index dedupe and write dedupe cache.\n857: \t// This is to ensure that index entries are replicated to all the boltdb files in ingesters flushing replicated data.\n858: \tif helps performance.\n866: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexQueriesCacheConfig = cache.Config{\n867: \t\t\tEmbeddedCache: cache.EmbeddedCacheConfig{\n868: \t\t\t\tEnabled:   true,\n869: \t\t\t\tMaxSizeMB: 200,\n870: \t\t\t\t// This is a small hack to save some CPU cycles.\n871: \t\t\t\t// We check if the object is still valid after pulling it from cache using the IndexCacheValidity value\n872: \t\t\t\t// however it has to be deserialized to do so, setting the cache validity to some arbitrary amount less than the\n873: \t\t\t\t// IndexCacheValidity guarantees the Embedded cache will expire the object first which can be done without\n874: \t\t\t\t// having to deserialize the object.\n875: \t\t\t\tTTL: t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity - 1*time.Minute,\n876: \t\t\t},\n877: \t\t}\n878: \n879: \t\t// We do not want ingester to unnecessarily keep downloading files\n880: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeWriteOnly\n881: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IngesterDBRetainPeriod = shipperQuerierIndexUpdateDelay(t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity, t.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.ResyncInterval)\n885: \n886: \tcase t.Cfg.isTarget(Querier), t.Cfg.isTarget(Ruler), t.Cfg.isTarget(Read), t.Cfg.isTarget(Backend), t.isModuleActive(IndexGateway), t.Cfg.isTarget(BloomPlanner), t.Cfg.isTarget(BloomBuilder):\n887: \t\t// We do not want query to do any updates to index\n888: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeReadOnly\n889: t.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.ResyncInterval)\n897: \t}\n898: }\n899: \n900: func (t *Loki) setupAsyncStore() error {\n901: \tvar asyncStore bool\n902: \n903: \tshipperConfigIdx := calculateMaxLookBack(pc config.PeriodConfig, maxLookBackConfig, minDuration time.Duration) (time.Duration, error) {\n1833: \tif pc.ObjectType != indexshipper.FilesystemObjectStoreType && maxLookBackConfig.Nanoseconds() != 0 {\n1834: \t\treturn 0, errors.New(\"it is an error to specify a non zero `query_store_max_look_back_period` value when using any object store other than not limit ingester queries from AsyncStore.\n1851: \tif queryIngestersWithinConfig == 0 {\n1852: \t\treturn 0\n1853: \t}\n1854: \n1855: \tif queryIngestersWithinConfig < minDuration {\n1856: \t\treturn minDuration\n1857: \t}\n1858: \treturn queryIngestersWithinConfig\n1859: }\n1860: \n1861: // shipperQuerierIndexUpdateDelay returns duration it could take for queriers to serve the index since it was uploaded.\n1862: // It considers upto 3 sync attempts for the indexgateway/queries to be successful in syncing the files to factor in worst case scenarios like\n1863: // failures in sync, low download throughput, various kinds of caches in between etc. which can delay the sync operation from getting all the updates from the storage.\n1864: // It also considers index cache validity because a querier could have cached index just before it was going to resync which means\n1865: // it would keep serving index until the cache entries expire.\n1866: func shipperQuerierIndexUpdateDelay(cacheValidity, resyncInterval time.Duration) time.Duration {\n1867: \treturn cacheValidity + resyncInterval*3\n1868: }\n1869: \n1870: // shipperIngesterIndexUploadDelay returns duration it could take for an index file containing id of a chunk to be uploaded to the shared store since it got flushed.\n1871: func shipperIngesterIndexUploadDelay() time.Duration {\n1872: \treturn boltdb.ShardDBsByDuration + indexshipper.UploadInterval\n1873: }\n1874: \n1875: // shipperMinIngesterQueryStoreDuration returns minimum duration(with some buffer) ingesters should query their stores to\n1876: // avoid missing any logs or chunk ids due to async nature of shipper.\n1877: func shipperMinIngesterQueryStoreDuration(maxChunkAge, querierUpdateDelay time.Duration) time.Duration {\n1878: \treturn maxChunkAge + shipperIngesterIndexUploadDelay() + querierUpdateDelay + 5*time.Minute\n1879: }\n1880: \n1881: // NewServerService constructs service from Server component.\n1882: // servicesToWaitFor is called when server is stopping, and should return all\n1883: // services that need to terminate before server actually stops.\n1884: // N.B.: this function is NOT Cortex specific, please let's keep it that way.\n1885: // Passed server should not react on signals. Early return from Run function is considered to be an error.\n1886: func NewServerService(serv *server.Server, servicesToWaitFor func() []services.Service) services.Service {\n1887: \tserverDone := make(chan error, 1)\n1888: \n1889: \trunFn := func(ctx context.Context) error {\n1890: \t\tgo func() {\n1891: \t\t\tdefer close(serverDone)\n1892: \t\t\tserverDone <- serv.Run()\n1893: \t\t}()\n1894: \n1895: \t\tselect {\n1896: \t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n1897: \t\t\treturn nil\n1898: \t\tcase err := <-serverDone:\n1899: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n1900: \t\t\t\treturn err\n1901: \t\t\t}\n1902: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"server stopped unexpectedly\")\n1903: \t\t}\n1904: \t}\n1905: \n1906: \tstoppingFn := func(_ error) error {\n1907: \t\t// wait until all modules are done, and then shutdown server.\n1908: \t\tfor _, s := range servicesToWaitFor() {\n1909: \t\t\t_ = s.AwaitTerminated(context.Background())\n1910: \t\t}\n1911: \n1912: \t\t// shutdown HTTP and gRPC servers (this also unblocks Run)\n1913: \t\tserv.Shutdown()\n1914: \n1915: \t\t// if not closed yet, wait until server stops.\n1916: \t\t<-serverDone\n1917: \t\tlevel.Info(util_log.Logger).Log(\"msg\", \"server stopped\")\n1918: \t\treturn nil\n1919: \t}\n1920: \n1921: \treturn services.NewBasicService(nil, runFn, stoppingFn)\n1922: }\n1923: \n1924: // DisableSignalHandling puts a dummy signal handler\n1925: func DisableSignalHandling(config *server.Config) {\n1926: \tconfig.SignalHandler = make(ignoreSignalHandler)\n1927: }\n1928: \n1929: type ignoreSignalHandler chan struct{}\n1930: \n1931: func (dh
